## <a name="windows-server-2003-r2"></a><span data-ttu-id="0d051-709">Windows Server 2003 R2</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0d051-709">Windows Server 2003 R2</span></span>

-   [<span data-ttu-id="0d051-710">Attribute</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0d051-710">Attributes</span></span>](#windows-server-2003-r2-attributes)

## <a name="windows-server-2008-attributes"></a><span data-ttu-id="0d051-1066">Windows Server 2008-Attribute</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0d051-1066">Windows Server 2008 Attributes</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="0d051-1067">Diese Klasse enthält die folgenden Attribute für Windows Server 2008:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0d051-1067">This class contains the following attributes for Windows Server 2008:</span></span>
